ASYNC LOADING RACE CONDITIONS\n\n#### Notifications Dropdown - Potential Race Condition\n**File:** `/workspace/public/src/client/header/notifications.js` (lines 9-10)\n\n```javascript\nnotifTrigger.on('show.bs.dropdown', (ev) => {\n    requireAndCall('loadNotifications', $(ev.target).parent().find('[component=\"notifications/list\"]'));\n});\n```\n\n**Issue:** \n- The `show.bs.dropdown` event fires when the dropdown is about to show, but there's **no guarantee** that async notification loading completes before Bootstrap renders the dropdown\n- The `loadNotifications` function uses `socket.emit()` with callbacks (line 33 in notifications.js), which is asynchronous\n- Bootstrap's dropdown positioning may happen before content is loaded, causing layout shift\n- The dropdown content is loaded via `app.parseAndTranslate()` which is also async (lines 43-70)\n\n#### Category Selector in Modal - Timing Issue\n**File:** `/workspace/public/src/modules/categorySelector.js` (lines 100-103)\n\n```javascript\nif (options.openOnLoad) {\n    modal.on('shown.bs.modal', function () {\n        modal.find('.dropdown-toggle').dropdown('toggle');\n    });\n}\n```\n\n**Critical Issue:** The dropdown is toggled in `shown.bs.modal` event, but `categorySearch.init()` sets up listeners on `show.bs.dropdown` (line 27 of categorySearch.js). The async content loading via `api.get()` (line 73) may not complete before Bootstrap tries to position the dropdown menu.\n\n### 2. DROPUP CLASS NOT REAPPLIED AFTER ASYNC CONTENT LOADS\n\n#### Post Tools and Thread Tools - Missing Update Calls\n**Files:** \n- `/workspace/public/src/client/topic/postTools.js` (lines 39-72)\n- `/workspace/public/src/client/topic/threadTools.js` (lines 207-222)\n\n**Pattern:**\n```javascript\ncontainer.on('show.bs.dropdown', '.thread-tools', async function () {\n    const $this = $(this);\n    const dropdownMenu = $this.find('.dropdown-menu');\n    const { top } = this.getBoundingClientRect();\n    $this.toggleClass('dropup', top > window.innerHeight / 2);  // Applied once on show\n    \n    if (dropdownMenu.attr('data-loaded')) {\n        return;\n    }\n    // ... async loading ...\n    dropdownMenu.attr('data-loaded', 'true').html(html);  // Content changes but dropup not rechecked\n});\n```\n\n**Issue:** \n- The `dropup` class is toggled based on viewport position **only when the dropdown opens**\n- After async content is loaded, if the page has scrolled or content has been injected, the dropdown position may be incorrect\n- The `dropup` class is never re-evaluated after async content loads\n- The placeholder content and final content may have different heights, causing position recalculation to be needed\n\n### 3. CATEGORY DROPDOWN IN MODALS - DROPUP CLASS PROBLEM\n\n**File:** `/workspace/public/src/modules/categorySelector.js` - modal implementation\n\n**Critical Issue:** When a category selector dropdown is opened inside a modal dialog:\n1. The modal constrains the viewport for the dropdown\n2. The `dropup` class logic (checking `top > window.innerHeight / 2`) doesn't account for modal positioning\n3. The dropdown may try to open downward even though it would overflow the modal\n4. No `dropup` class management exists in `categorySearch.js` or `categorySelector.js`\n\n**Compare to working pattern in postTools.js:**\n```javascript\n$this.toggleClass('dropup', top > window.innerHeight / 2);\n```\n\nCategory selector does NOT have this logic at all.\n\n### 4. BOOTSTRAP DROPDOWN UPDATE() CALLS - PARTIAL IMPLEMENTATION\n\n**Files where `.update()` is called:**\n- `/workspace/public/src/modules/categorySearch.js` (lines 104-107) ✓ Correct\n- `/workspace/public/src/modules/tagFilter.js` (lines 177-180) ✓ Correct\n\n```javascript\nconst bsDropdown = bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance(el.find('.dropdown-toggle').get(0));\nif (bsDropdown) {\n    bsDropdown.update();\n}\n```\n\n**Issue:** This pattern is **inconsistently applied**:\n- `categorySearch.js` calls `.update()` after rendering async content ✓\n- `tagFilter.js` calls `.update()` after rendering async content ✓\n- `postTools.js` and `threadTools.js` DO NOT call `.update()` after async content loads ✗\n- `categorySelector.js` has no `.update()` call for modal dropdowns ✗\n\n### 5. ASYNC LOADING IN categorySearch.js - BEST PRACTICE FOUND\n\n**File:** `/workspace/public/src/modules/categorySearch.js` (lines 72-109)\n\nThis is the **most correct implementation** in the codebase:\n\n```javascript\nfunction loadList(search, callback) {\n    api.get('/search/categories', {...}, function (err, { categories }) {\n        if (err) return alerts.error(err);\n        callback(localCategories.concat(categories));\n    });\n}\n\nfunction renderList(categories) {\n    // ... render HTML ...\n    app.parseAndTranslate(options.template, {...}, function (html) {\n        el.find('[component=\"category/list\"]').html(html.find('[component=\"category/list\"]').html());\n        \n        // CORRECT: Call update() after async content loads\n        const bsDropdown = bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance(el.find('.dropdown-toggle').get(0));\n        if (bsDropdown) {\n            bsDropdown.update();  // Recalculates positioning\n        }\n    });\n}\n```\n\nThis pattern should be replicated in other async dropdowns.\n\n### 6. NOTIFICATIONS DROPDOWN - MISSING PATTERN\n\n**File:** `/workspace/public/src/modules/notifications.js` (lines 31-72)\n\n```javascript\nNotifications.loadNotifications = function (notifList, callback) {\n    socket.emit('notifications.get', null, function (err, data) {\n        // ... data processing ...\n        app.parseAndTranslate('partials/notifications_list', { notifications }, function (html) {\n            notifList.html(html);\n            // ... click handlers ...\n            callback();\n        });\n    });\n};\n```\n\n**Issue:** \n- After `notifList.html(html)` updates the content, there's NO call to `bootstrap.Dropdown.getInstance().update()`\n- The dropdown position is never recalculated after async content loads\n- This can cause the dropdown menu to be misaligned relative to its final content\n\n### 7. KNOWN BOOTSTRAP 5 BEHAVIOR\n\nBootstrap 5 Dropdown API facts:\n- `show.bs.dropdown` fires BEFORE dropdown menu is shown\n- `shown.bs.dropdown` fires AFTER dropdown menu is shown\n- Content changes after `shown` event require `.update()` to recalculate Popper.js positioning\n- `.update()` must be called on the Dropdown instance, not the element\n- Modals have their own z-index stacking that can affect dropdown positioning\n\n### 8.
